ğŸ’¡ How to Contribute?

[27/04/24, 11:06:51â€¯AM] ~â€¯Amit Kumar Yadav: c++ solution class Solution {
  public:
    // Function to sort the given doubly linked list using Merge Sort.
    struct Node *sortDoubly(struct Node *head) {
        if(head == NULL)
           return head;
        Node *temp = head;
        vector<int> arr;
        while(temp != nullptr){
            arr.push_back(temp->data);
            temp = temp->next;        
        }
        sort(arr.begin(), arr.end());
        struct Node *newNode = new Node(arr[0]);
        struct Node *dummyHead = newNode;
        for(int i = 1; i < arr.size(); i++){
            Node *temp_node = new Node(arr[i]);
            dummyHead->next = temp_node;
            temp_node->prev = dummyHead;
            dummyHead = temp_node;
        }
        return newNode;
    }
};

[29/05/24, 9:03:51â€¯AM] ~â€¯Krishna Jadhav: int solve(int currnum,vector<int>&store,int n){
        if(currnum == n){
            return 0;
        }
        if(currnum > n){
            return INT_MAX; 
        }
        if(store[currnum]!=-1){
            return store[currnum];
        }
        int afteradd = solve(currnum + 1,store,n);
        if(currnum == 0){
            store[currnum] = afteradd+1;
            return store[currnum];
        }
        int afterdouble = solve(2*currnum,store,n);
        store[currnum] = min(afteradd,afterdouble)+1;
        return store[currnum];
    }
    int minOperation(int n)
    {
        int currnum = 0;
        vector<int>store(n,-1);
        return solve(currnum,store,n);
    }

[26/06/24, 11:04:02â€¯AM] ~â€¯Aditya Gaur: Certainly, here's a sample project proposal for an Attendance Portal Website:

---

# Project Proposal: Attendance Portal Website

## Introduction

The Attendance Portal Website project aims to create a comprehensive and user-friendly platform for managing attendance records in an educational institution. This web-based system will serve various user roles, including administrators, faculty members, students, the Dean, and Heads of Departments (HODs). The system will allow for efficient attendance recording, data management, and communication between different stakeholders.

## Project Objectives

The primary objectives of this project are as follows:

1. **Automated Attendance Management:** Develop an automated attendance tracking system to streamline the process of recording and managing attendance for students.

2. **User-Friendly Interface:** Create an intuitive web interface for easy login, attendance tracking, and data retrieval by various users.

3. **Role-Based Access Control:** Implement role-based access control to ensure that only authorized users can perform specific actions within the system.

4. **Data Security:** Prioritize the security of sensitive data, including personal information, attendance records, and user credentials.

5. **Efficient Communication:** Enable efficient communication between faculty, students, and administrative personnel for attendance-related matters.

6. **Notification System:** Implement a notification system to keep users informed about updates, notices, and important events.

## Project Components

The project will consist of the following key components:

### 1. 0-Level Data Flow Diagram (DFD)
- An overview of the system and its main stakeholders.

### 2. User Roles
- Administrator, Dean, HODs, Faculty, and Students, each with specific permissions and actions.

### 3. Administrative Portal
- Allows administrators to manage user accounts, handle requests, and monitor system operations.

### 4. HOD Portal
- Enables HODs to manage faculty, assign subjects, and view departmental attendance data.

### 5. Faculty Portal
- Allows faculty to take attendance, view assigned subjects, and communicate with students.

### 6. Dean Portal
- Provides access to Deans for viewing all assigned subjects, managing attendance, and personal information.

### 7. Student Portal
- Enables students to view attendance data, subject information, and receive notifications.

### 8. Database Management
- Backend databases for storing user data, attendance records, and communication data.

### 9. Notification System
- An integrated notification system for sending and receiving important updates.

## Methodology

We will follow the Agile project management methodology to ensure flexibility, collaboration, and iterative development. Regular meetings and feedback sessions with stakeholders will be held to incorporate changes and updates as needed.

## Timeline

The project will be divided into phases, each with its deliverables and timelines:

- Phase 1: Requirement Analysis and System Design (Month 1-2)
- Phase 2: Development and Testing (Month 3-6)
- Phase 3: User Training and Pilot Testing (Month 7-8)
- Phase 4: Deployment and Maintenance (Month 9 onwards)

## Budget

The estimated budget for this project includes costs for development, testing, hardware, software licenses, and maintenance. A detailed budget breakdown will be provided in the project plan.

## Conclusion

The Attendance Portal Website project is a crucial system for the efficient management of attendance records in our educational institution. We believe that by implementing this system, we will improve data accuracy, enhance communication, and simplify administrative tasks related to attendance. We look forward to your approval and support for the successful execution of this project.

If you have any questions or require further information, please do not hesitate to contact us.

---

This project proposal outlines the objectives, components, methodology, timeline, and budget for the Attendance Portal Website project. Adjustments can be made based on specific requirements and expectations.
